<script>

    $('.dropdown-title-left').click(function (event) {

        var $subMenu = $(this).next('.sub-menu');

        if ($subMenu.is(':hidden')) {
            $subMenu.slideDown();
        } else {
            $subMenu.slideUp();
        }
    });

    $(".dropdown-title-level-2").click(function (event) {
        var $subMenu = $(this).next('.sub-menu-level-2');

        if ($subMenu.is(':hidden')) {
            $subMenu.slideDown();
        } else {
            $subMenu.slideUp();
        }
    });
</script>

<script>
    let modalOpen = false;

    $(document).ready(function () {

        $("#regist-now-header").click(function () {
            if (!CommonModule.isLoggedIn() || CommonModule.isLoggedInMobile()) {
                window.location.href = "/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi"
            }
            else {
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/Users/CheckIsBrokerUserLogin',
                    type: 'GET',
                    success: function (data) {
                        if (data) {
                            if (data.status) {
                                if (data.url != "") {
                                    window.location.href = data.url
                                }
                                else {
                                    window.location.href = "/dang-ki-moi-gioi"
                                }
                            }
                            else {
                                window.location.href = "/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi"
                            }
                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = "/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi"
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        $("#btnDangTin").click(function () {
            var isLoggedInTVPL = CommonModule.getCookie("tvpl_access_token");
            var isLoggedInGG = CommonModule.getCookie("google_access_token");
            var isLoggedIn = CommonModule.getCookie("token");

            if (!isLoggedIn && !isLoggedInTVPL && !isLoggedInGG) {
                loginModalBinding();
                $(".modal-login").modal({
                    closable: false
                }).modal('show');
            } else {
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/Users/CheckExistPhoneUser",
                    type: "GET",
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.check) {
                            window.location.href = "/dang-tin";

                        } else {

                            $(".form-regist").show();
                            $(".form-login").hide();
                            $("#lable-welcome").text("Xác minh số điện thoại");
                            $("#login-footer").hide();
                            $(".lable-hello").hide();
                            $(".register").hide();
                            $("#verity-type").val(2);
                            $('.ui.modal.modal-login').modal({
                                closable: false
                            }).modal('show');
                        }
                    },
                    error: function () {
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        $("#btn-dangtin-mobile").click(function () {
            var isLoggedInTVPL = CommonModule.getCookie("tvpl_access_token");
            var isLoggedInGG = CommonModule.getCookie("google_access_token");
            var isLoggedIn = CommonModule.getCookie("token");

            if (!isLoggedIn && !isLoggedInTVPL && !isLoggedInGG) {
                loginModalBinding();
                $('.ui.sidebar').sidebar('hide');
                $(".modal-login").modal({
                    closable: false
                }).modal('show');
            }
            else {
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/Users/CheckExistPhoneUser",
                    type: "GET",
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.check) {
                            window.location.href = "/dang-tin";
                        } else {
                            //$("#modal-add-phone").modal({
                            //    closable: false
                            //}).modal('show');
                            $(".form-regist").show();
                            $(".form-login").hide();
                            $("#lable-welcome").text("Xác minh số điện thoại");
                            $("#login-footer").hide();
                            $(".lable-hello").hide();
                            $(".register").hide();
                            $("#verity-type").val(2);
                            $('.ui.modal.modal-login').modal({
                                closable: false
                            }).modal('show');
                        }
                    },
                    error: function () {
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        $('#right-icon-add-phone').on('click', function () {
            const $passwordInput = $('#password-add');
            const isPasswordVisible = $passwordInput.attr('type') === 'text';

            $passwordInput.attr('type', isPasswordVisible ? 'password' : 'text');
            $(this).toggleClass('eye').toggleClass('eye slash');
        });
        $('.ui.dropdown').dropdown();

        $('.dropdown-title').on('click', function (text, value, element) {
            event.preventDefault();
            const href = $(this).attr('href');
            if (href) {
                window.location.href = href;
            }
        });

        $(window).resize();
        $('.close').on('click', function () {
            $('.ui.sidebar').sidebar('hide');
            $("#menu-left-mobile").show();

            $("#navigation-bar-bottom").fadeIn(500);
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($(this).scrollTop() > 100) {
                $('#backToTop').fadeIn();
            } else {
                $('#backToTop').fadeOut();
            }
        });
        $('#backToTop').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, '300');
        });

        function toggleIconButtons() {
            if ($('.user-sign-in').css('display') === 'block') {
                //$('.icon-button').css('display', 'block');
                $('.login-divider-header').css('display', 'none');
                //$('#content-login').css('justify-content', 'flex-end');
            } else {
                //$('.icon-button').css('display', 'none');
                $('.login-divider-header').css('display', 'block');
                //$('#content-login').css('justify-content', 'flex-end');
            }
        }

        // Initial check when the page loads
        toggleIconButtons();

        // Dynamically check when `.user-sign-in` visibility changes
        // MutationObserver is ideal for monitoring style changes
        const observer = new MutationObserver(toggleIconButtons);
        observer.observe(document.querySelector('.user-sign-in'), { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['style'] });

        // Optional: Attach click or other events to force the check
        $('.user-sign-in').on('click', toggleIconButtons());


        //set logo on top when mobile tablet mode
        if (isMobile_TabletMode) {
            $('.logo-mobile-version').attr('style', 'display:block !important');
        }

        document.addEventListener("scroll", function () {
            const header = document.getElementById("header");
            const img = document.getElementById("logo-img");
            const text = document.getElementsByClassName("icon-button__badge");
            const headerContainer = document.getElementsByClassName("header-container");
            const $projectSearchbar = document.getElementById("project-search-bar");
            const searchBarSale = document.getElementsByClassName("searchBarSale");
            const menuTop = document.getElementsByClassName("menu-top");
            const banDemo = document.getElementById("ban-demo");

            for (let i = 0; i < text.length; i++) {
                if (window.scrollY > 2) {
                    text[i].style.fontSize = "10px";
                    text[i].style.height = "15px";
                    text[i].style.width = "15px";
                    text[i].style.top = "-6px";
                    text[i].style.right = "-2px";
                } else {
                    text[i].style.fontSize = "14px";
                    text[i].style.height = "20px";
                    text[i].style.width = "20px";
                }
            }

            if (window.scrollY > 2) {
                header.classList.add("shrink");
                //headerContainer[0].style.padding = "0 10px";
                img.style.width = "64px";
                img.style.height = "64px";

                if ($projectSearchbar) $projectSearchbar.style.paddingTop = "60px";

                if (searchBarSale.length > 0) {
                    searchBarSale[0].style.paddingTop = "68px";

        function getZoomLevel() {
            return window.devicePixelRatio;
        }

            let lastScrollTop = 0;
            const searchContainer = document.querySelector('.mobile-container-scroll');
            searchContainer.style.display = 'block';


            window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
                const logo = document.querySelector('.mobile-logo-scroll');
                const searchScroll = document.querySelector('.mobile-search-scroll');
                const mobileHeader = document.querySelector('.mobile-header');
                const mobileLogo = document.querySelector('.logo-mobile-version');
                const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;


                if (scrollTop > 50) {
                    // Scroll xuống
                    logo.style.display = 'none';
                    searchContainer.style.display = 'none';
                    searchScroll.style.display = 'block';
                    mobileHeader.style.width = '100%';
                    mobileLogo.style.width = '80%';
                } else {
                    // Scroll lên
                    logo.style.display = 'flex';
                    searchContainer.style.display = 'block';
                    searchScroll.style.display = 'none';
                    mobileHeader.style.width = '100%';
                    mobileLogo.style.width = 'auto';
                }

                lastScrollTop = scrollTop <= 0 ? 0 : scrollTop;
            });

        $.fn.form.settings.rules.validPhoneForm = function (value) {
            if (value) {
                return CommonModule.isValidPhoneNumber(value);
            }
            else return true;
        }
        $.fn.form.settings.rules.validPasswordForm = function (value) {
            if (value) {
                return CommonModule.isValidPassword(value);
            }
            else return true;
        };
        $.fn.form.settings.rules.validCheckExistPhone = function (value) {
            if (value) {
                var isPhoneValid = false;
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/Users/CheckExistUser",
                    type: 'POST',
                    dataType: "json",
                    method: "POST",
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    data: JSON.stringify({ PhoneNumber: value }),
                    async: false,
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.result.Success) {
                            isPhoneValid = false;
                        } else {
                            isPhoneValid = true;
                        }
                    },
                    error: function () {
                        isPhoneValid = false;
                    }
                });
                return isPhoneValid;
            } else {
                return true;
            }
        };


        $("#form-add-phone")
            .form({
                fields: {
                    phoneAdd: {
                        identifier: 'phoneAdd',
                        rules: [
                            {
                                type: 'empty',
                                prompt: 'Vui lòng nhập số điện thoại'
                            },
                            {
                                type: 'validPhoneForm',
                                prompt: 'Vui lòng nhập số điện thoại hợp lệ'
                            },
                            {
                                type: 'validCheckExistPhone',
                                prompt: 'Số điện thoại này đã được đăng ký. Vui lòng dùng số điện thoại khác để đăng ký.'
                            }
                        ]
                    },
                    passwordAdd: {
                        identifier: 'passwordAdd',
                        rules: [
                            {
                                type: 'empty',
                                prompt: 'Vui lòng nhập mật khẩu'
                            },
                            {
                                type: 'validPasswordForm',
                                prompt: 'Mật khẩu phải có tối thiểu 8 ký tự. Trong đó: có chứa đầy đủ chữ cái viết thường, viết hoa, ký tự đặc biệt và ký tự số!'
                            }
                        ]
                    },
                },
                onSuccess: function (event, fields) {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    var validpass = CommonModule.isValidPassword(fields.passwordAdd);
                    var validphone = CommonModule.isValidPhoneNumber(fields.phoneAdd);
                    if (!validpass || !validphone) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var dataInput = {
                        phone: fields.phoneAdd,
                        password: fields.passwordAdd,
                    };

                    $.ajax({
                        url: '/Users/UpdatePhoneToUser',
                        type: 'POST',
                        data: dataInput,
                        success: function (data) {
                            if (data) {
                                $("#modal-add-phone").modal('hide');
                                $("#phone-add").val("");
                                $("#password-add").val("");
                                CommonModule.showToast("Success", "Cập nhật số điện thoại và mật khẩu thành công.", "success");
                                window.location.href = "/dang-tin";
                            } else {
                                CommonModule.showToast("Error", "Có lỗi xảy ra khi gửi mail.", "error");
                            }
                        },
                        error: function () {
                            CommonModule.showToast("Error", "Có lỗi xảy ra khi gửi mail.", "error");
                        }
                    });
                }
            })
        $('#phone-add').on('input', function () {
            var $errorMessageContainer = $("#error-msg-add-phone");
            var phone = $(this).val();
            var isValidPhone = CommonModule.isValidPhoneNumber(phone);
            $errorMessageContainer.find('ul li').each(function () {
                if (!$(this).hasClass('phone-error') && !$(this).hasClass('password-error')) {
                    $(this).remove();
                }
            });
            if ($errorMessageContainer.find('ul').length === 0) {
                $errorMessageContainer.append('<ul class="list"></ul>');
            }
            if (!isValidPhone) {
                if ($errorMessageContainer.find('ul li.phone-error').length === 0) {
                    $errorMessageContainer.find('ul').append('<li class="phone-error">Vui lòng nhập số điện thoại hợp lệ</li>');
                }
                $errorMessageContainer.show();
            } else {
                $errorMessageContainer.find('ul li.phone-error').remove();
                if ($errorMessageContainer.find('ul li').length === 0) {
                    $errorMessageContainer.hide();
                }
            }
        });
        $('#password-add').on('input', function () {
            var $errorMessageContainer = $("#error-msg-add-phone");
            var password = $(this).val();
            var isValidPassword = CommonModule.isValidPassword(password);
            $errorMessageContainer.find('ul li').each(function () {
                if (!$(this).hasClass('phone-error') && !$(this).hasClass('password-error')) {
                    $(this).remove();
                }
            });
            if ($errorMessageContainer.find('ul').length === 0) {
                $errorMessageContainer.append('<ul class="list"></ul>');
            }
            if (!isValidPassword) {
                if ($errorMessageContainer.find('ul li.password-error').length === 0) {
                    $errorMessageContainer.find('ul').append('<li class="password-error">Mật khẩu phải có tối thiểu 8 ký tự. Trong đó: có chứa đầy đủ chữ cái viết thường, viết hoa, ký tự đặc biệt và ký tự số!</li>');
                }
                $errorMessageContainer.show();
            } else {
                $errorMessageContainer.find('ul li.password-error').remove();
                if ($errorMessageContainer.find('ul li').length === 0) {
                    $errorMessageContainer.hide();
                }
            }
        });
        $("#form-add-phone").submit(function () {
            if ($("#error-msg-add-phone").find('ul li').length > 0) $("#error-msg-add-phone").show();
        });

        $("#valid-email").on("blur", function () {
            if ($(this).val().trim() != "") {
                if (!CommonModule.isValidTaxCode($(this).val().trim())) {
                    $("#error-msg-valid-email").text("Vui lòng nhập mã số thuế hợp lệ").show();

                }

                    //        check_valid_email = false;

                    //});
                }
            }
        });
        $("#form-valid-email").on("submit", function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            $("#loading-sendmail-valid").show();
            var taxcode = $("#valid-email").val().trim();
            if (taxcode = "" || !check_valid_email) {
                $("#loading-sendmail-valid").hide();
                return;
            }
            else {
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/Users/UpdateOrValidTaxCode",
                    type: "POST",
                    dataType: "json",
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    data: JSON.stringify({ taxcode: $("#valid-email").val().trim() }),
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.Success) {
                            $("#loading-sendmail-valid").hide();
                            $("#modal-valid-email").modal('hide');
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#loading-sendmail-valid").hide();
                            $("#error-msg-valid-email").text(response.Message).show();
                        }
                    },
                    error: function () {
                        $("#loading-sendmail-valid").hide();
                        $("#error-msg-valid-email").text("Hệ thống đang gián đoạn, vui lòng thử lại sau!").show();
                    }
                });
            }
        });
        $("#form-valid-email").form();
        $('#modal-valid-email .close').click(function () {
            $("#valid-email").val("")
            $("#error-msg-valid-email").hide();
            $("#content-valid").show();
            $("#content-submit").hide();
            $.ajax({
                url: "/Users/UpdateOrValidTaxCode",
                type: "POST",
                dataType: "json",
                contentType: "application/json",
                data: JSON.stringify({ taxcode: $("#valid-email").val().trim() }),
                success: function (response) {
                    if (response.Success) {
                        $("#loading-sendmail-valid").hide();
                        $("#content-valid").hide();
                        $("#content-submit").show();
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#loading-sendmail-valid").hide();
                    }
                },
                error: function () {
                    $("#loading-sendmail-valid").show();
                }
            });
        });
        $("#modal-login-sigin-fast .close").click(function () {
            $("#content-regist-fast").css("display", "block");
            $("#verify-OTP-fast").css("display", "none");
            $("#verify-OTP-success-fast").css("display", "none");
            $("#phone-regist-fast").val("");
            $("#error-form-regist-fast").text("").hide();
            $('.mini-input-fast input').val('');
            clearInterval(timerInterval);
            timerInterval = null;
            $('#timer-fast').text('').hide();
        });

    });
    function CheckExistUser(phone) {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/Users/CheckExistUser",
            type: 'POST',
            dataType: "json",
            method: "POST",
            contentType: "application/json",
            data: JSON.stringify({ PhoneNumber: phone }),
            success: function (response) {
                if (response.result.Success) {
                    existPhone = true;
                    return false;
                } else {
                    existPhone = false
                    return true;
                }
            },
            error: function () {
                existPhone = true;
                return false;
            }
        });
    }
    var timerInterval = null;
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('#loai-van-ban').dropdown();
        $('#co-quan-ban-hanh').dropdown();
        $('#linh-vuc').dropdown();

        $('#ban-hanh-tu, #ban-hanh-den, #hieu-luc-tu, #hieu-luc-den').calendar({
            type: 'date',

            formatter: {
                date: function (date, settings) {
                    if (!(date instanceof Date) || isNaN(date.getTime())) return '';
                    const day = date.getDate().toString().padStart(2, '0');
                    const month = (date.getMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0');
                    const year = date.getFullYear();
                    return `${day}/${month}/${year}`;
                }
            },

            parser: {
                date: function (text, settings) {
                    if (!text) return null;
                    const parts = text.split('/');
                    if (parts.length !== 3) return null;
                    const day = parseInt(parts[0], 10);
                    const month = parseInt(parts[1], 10) - 1;
                    const year = parseInt(parts[2], 10);
                    if (isNaN(day) || isNaN(month) || isNaN(year)) return null;
                    return new Date(year, month, day);
                }
            }
        });



        const STORAGE_KEY = 'moRongTimKiem';
        const $section = $('#tim-nang-cao');
        const $toggleBtn = $('#btThemDieuKien');
        const $icon = $toggleBtn.find('i');
        const $text = $toggleBtn.find('.text-label');

        const isOpen = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) === 'true';

        if (isOpen) {
            $section.show();
            $icon.removeClass('plus').addClass('minus');
            $text.text('Bớt điều kiện');
        } else {
            $section.hide();
            $icon.removeClass('minus').addClass('plus');
            $text.text('Thêm điều kiện');
        }

        $toggleBtn.on('click', function () {
            if ($section.is(':visible')) {
                $section.slideUp();
                $icon.removeClass('minus').addClass('plus');
                $text.text('Thêm điều kiện');
                localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, 'false');
            } else {
                $section.slideDown();
                $icon.removeClass('plus').addClass('minus');
                $text.text('Bớt điều kiện');
                localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, 'true');
            }
        });


        tippy('.noti-pro', {
            content: "Tiện ích dành riêng cho tài khoản TVPL Pro",
            theme: 'light-border'
        });

        tippy('.noti-basic-pro', {
            content: "Tiện ích dành riêng cho tài khoản TVPL Basic và TVPL Pro",
            theme: 'light-border'
        });


    });
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $("#button-submit-vb-tvpl").click(function (event) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var username = $("#username-vb-tvpl").val().trim();
            var password = $("#password-vb-tvpl").val().trim();

            if (!username || !password) {
                $("#error-msg-vb-tvpl").text("Tên đăng nhập hoặc mật khẩu không được để trống");
                return;
            }
            else {
                $("#error-msg-vb-tvpl").text("");
                var data = {
                    username: username,
                    password: password,
                    rememberMe: true,
                    returnUrl: window.location.href
                }
                $.ajax({
                    url: "/signin-tvpl",
                    method: "POST",
                    contentType: "application/json",
                    dataType: "json",
                    data: JSON.stringify(data),
                    success: function (response) {
                        if (response.success != false) {
                            window.location.href = response.urlResponse;
                            $(".login").hide();
                            $('.login-bar-header').attr("style", "margin-top: 8px;");
                            $("#user-login").text((!response.fullname || response.fullname.trim() === "") ? response.username : response.fullname).show();
                            $("#user-login-mobile").text((!response.fullname || response.fullname.trim() === "") ? response.username : response.fullname).show();
                            $(".user-avatar").attr("src", (!response.urlImage || response.urlImage.trim() === "") ? 'https://cdn.thuviennhadat.vn/upload/bds/HomePage/avatar_7610196.png' : response.urlImage);
                            $(".user-sign-in").css({
                                "display": "block",
                                "padding-right": "10px",
                                "padding-left": "10px",
                            });
                            $("#form-dimmer").removeClass("active");

                            CommonModule.showToast("", "Đăng nhập thành công", "success");
                            //closeModal();
                            //$("#modal-login-tvpl").modal("hide");
                            //isStillLoggedIn = true;
                        }
                        else {
                            $("#error-msg-vb-tvpl").text(response.message);
                        }
                    },
                    error: function () {
                        console.log("Login Failed");
                    }
                });
            }
        });

    });
</script>        </div>

<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
    $(document).ready(function () {


     
        // Hàm tạo cookie
        function setCookie(name, value, days) {
            var expires = "";
            if (days) {
                var date = new Date();
                date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
            }
            document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
        }

        // Hàm đọc cookie
        function getCookie(name) {
            var nameEQ = name + "=";
            var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
            }
            return null;
        }

        // Xử lý sự kiện khi nhấn nút "Tôi đã hiểu"
        $('#btnHieuLawnet').on('click', function () {
            $('#mdThongBaoLawnet').modal('hide');
            setCookie("lawnetDismissed", "1", 30); // Lưu cookie trong 30 ngày
        });

        // Kiểm tra cookie trước khi hiển thị modal
        setTimeout(function () {
            var hasVBPL = window.location.pathname.includes("/vbpl");
            var searchParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            var fromLawnet = searchParams.get("ref") === "lawnet";
            var dismissed = getCookie("lawnetDismissed");

            if (hasVBPL && fromLawnet && !dismissed) {
                $('#mdThongBaoLawnet').modal({
                    closable: false,
                    autofocus: true
                }).modal('show');
            }
        }, 2000);
       






        var x = $(window).width();
        StickyPage(x);
    });


    $("#btnVanBan").click(function () {
        window.location.href = window.location.href + 'vbpl';
    });
    $('.menu .item').tab();
    $('.menu .item').on('click', function () {
        var tab = $(this).attr('data-tab');

        if (tab === 'tk_tab_3') {
            $("#type").val(3);
            $("#tukhoa").attr("placeholder", "Tìm kiếm công văn pháp luật");
        } else if (tab === 'tk_tab_2') {
            $("#type").val(99);
            $("#tukhoa").attr("placeholder", "Tìm kiếm dự thảo pháp luật");
        }
        else if (tab === 'tk_tab_4') {
            $("#type").val(99);
            $("#tukhoa").attr("placeholder", "Tìm kiếm Tiêu chuẩn Việt Nam");
        }

        else {
            $("#type").val(null);
            $("#tukhoa").attr("placeholder", "Tìm kiếm văn bản pháp luật");
        }
    });
    function StickyPage(x) {
        if (x > 991) {

            setTimeout(
                function () {
                    var l = $("#dvTrungTam").height();
                    var r = $("#dvSubLeft").height();

                    if (l < r) {
                       
                    }
                    else {
                        $("#dvSubLeft").stick_in_parent({
                            offset_top: 80
                        });

                        $("#dvCamNangNhaDatTrangChuVanBan").stick_in_parent({
                            offset_top: 80
                        });
                    }
                }
                , 500);

        }
    }

</script>

<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        const path = window.location.pathname;

        const slug = path.split("/")[1] || "";
        const match = path.match(/-([0-9]+)\.html$/);
        const postId = match ? match[1] : "";

        if (!slug || !postId) return;

        const content = `tuganlink.${slug}.${postId}`;

        document.querySelectorAll('#main-content a[href]').forEach(function (a) {
            // ❌ Bỏ qua nếu nằm trong .slide_inbv
            if (a.closest('.slide_inbv')) return;

            const href = a.getAttribute('href');
            if (!href) return;

            if (
                !href.includes('thuviennhadat.vn/ban-') &&
                !href.includes('thuviennhadat.vn/cho-thue-')
            ) return;

            const url = new URL(href, window.location.origin);

            url.searchParams.set(
                "utm_source",
                "thuviennhadat_trangthongtin_noidung"
            );
            url.searchParams.set("utm_medium", "internal");
            url.searchParams.set("utm_campaign", "rao_vat_tu_trang_thong_tin");
            url.searchParams.set("utm_content", content);

            a.href = url.toString();
        });
    });
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var regisStatus = localStorage.getItem("tvnd-register-requirement-status");
        var regisShowDate = localStorage.getItem("tvnd-register-requirement-date");

        if (regisStatus == 'active') {
            activeContainerRegisterRequirement();
        }
        else {
            hiddenContainerRegisterRequirement();
        }

        $('#container-register-requirement .btn-close').on('click', function () {
            deactiveContainerRegisterRequirement();
        });

        $('#container-register-requirement .tag-name').on('click', function () {
            activeContainerRegisterRequirement();
        });

        $('#modal-open-register-requirement .button').on('click', function () {
            deactiveContainerRegisterRequirement();
        });

        setTimeout(() => {
            triggerActiveContainerRegisterRequirement();
        }, 20000);
    });

    function triggerActiveContainerRegisterRequirement() {
        var regisShowDate = localStorage.getItem("tvnd-register-requirement-date");
        if (!regisShowDate || parseInt(regisShowDate) <= Date.now()) {
            $('#container-register-requirement').addClass('active');
            $('#container-register-requirement img').addClass('animation-zoom');
            localStorage.setItem("tvnd-register-requirement-status", "active");
        }
    }

    function activeContainerRegisterRequirement() {
        $('#container-register-requirement').addClass('active');
        $('#container-register-requirement img').addClass('animation-zoom');
        localStorage.setItem("tvnd-register-requirement-status", "active");
    }

    function hiddenContainerRegisterRequirement() {
        $('#container-register-requirement').removeClass('active');
        $('#container-register-requirement img').removeClass('animation-zoom');
        localStorage.setItem("tvnd-register-requirement-status", "deactive");
    }

    function deactiveContainerRegisterRequirement() {
        $('#container-register-requirement').removeClass('active');
        $('#container-register-requirement img').removeClass('animation-zoom');
        localStorage.setItem("tvnd-register-requirement-status", "deactive");

        completedContainerRegisterRequirement();
    }

    function completedContainerRegisterRequirement() {
        let dateNow = new Date();
        localStorage.setItem("tvnd-register-requirement-date", dateNow.setDate(dateNow.getDate() + 1));
    }

    function openModalRegisterRequirement() {
        $('#modal-open-register-requirement').modal({
            inverted: true,
            //onHidden: function () {
            //    deactiveContainerRegisterRequirement();
            //}
        }).modal('show');
    }
</script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {

        $('#main-content img').each(function () {
            var src = $(this).attr('src');
            if (src && src.includes('luatnhadat.vn')) {
                $(this).attr('src', src.replace('luatnhadat.vn', 'thuviennhadat.vn'));
            }
        });

        $('#main-content a').each(function () {
            var href = $(this).attr('href');
            if (href && href.includes('luatnhadat.vn')) {
                $(this).attr('href', href.replace('luatnhadat.vn', 'thuviennhadat.vn'));
            }
        });

        $('.lazy').lazy({
            effect: "fadeIn",
            effectTime: 2000,
            threshold: 0
        });
        $('#broker-now').click(function () {
            if (!CommonModule.isLoggedIn() || CommonModule.isLoggedInMobile()) {
                window.location.href = "/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi"
            }
            else {
                $.ajax({
                    url: '/Users/CheckIsBrokerUserLogin',
                    type: 'GET',
                    success: function (data) {
                        if (data) {
                            if (data.status) {
                                if (data.url != "") {
                                    window.location.href = data.url
                                }
                                else {
                                    window.location.href = "/dang-ki-moi-gioi"
                                }
                            }
                            else {
                                window.location.href = "/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi"
                            }
                        }
                        else {
                            window.location.href = "/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi"
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        //chỉ cho zoom ở 1 số trang
        const flexibleZoomPages = [
            '/huong-dan-dac-diem-dang-tin',
            '/chuyen-trang-moi-gioi',
        ];

        const path = window.location.pathname;

        const allowZoom = flexibleZoomPages.some(url => path.startsWith(url));

        setZoom(allowZoom);
    });

    // Function to open Tawk.to chat
    function openTawkChat() {
        if (typeof Tawk_API !== 'undefined' && Tawk_API.maximize) {
            Tawk_API.maximize(); // Opens the Tawk.to chat
        } else {
            console.log("Tawk.to script is not loaded yet.");
        }
    }

    function setZoom(enabled) {
        const meta = document.querySelector('meta[name="viewport"]');
        if (!meta) return;

        if (enabled) {
            meta.setAttribute('content', 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=5.0, user-scalable=yes');
        } else {
            meta.setAttribute('content', 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0, maximum-scale=1.0, user-scalable=no');
        }
    }

    function openPopupNewUser() {
        if (!(window.location.pathname === "/tai-khoan/thong-tin-ca-nhan") && !isOnlyMobileMode) {
            Swal.fire({
                position: "top-end",
                title: "<div style='font-size: 13px;'>Chào mừng bạn đến với <span class='brand-name' style='padding-top:0; font-size: 14px;'><span class='br-1'>Thư Viện</span> <span class='br-2'>Nhà Đất</span></span></div>",
                html: "<div style='font-size: 12px;'>Quý khách vui lòng truy cập <span><a style='color: red;' href='/tai-khoan/thong-tin-ca-nhan?type=1'>tại đây</a></span> để cập nhật thông tin cá nhân tài khoản!</div>",
                showConfirmButton: false,
                focusConfirm: false,
                allowOutsideClick: true,
                timer: 10000,
                customClass: {
                    popup: 'swal-small-newuser'
                }
            });
        }
    }

</script>
